## Page 47

-43-

Challenge for the 2 S--

INDECISION. WHICH WAY?

Birthdates Ruled by the 2 S

Jan.12.
Cap.

Feb.10.
Aquar,

Mar. 8.
Pisc.

Ruler- Saturn.

There is no laziness in

this birthdate, but rather
a willingness to work hard
--often too hard~- to at-
tain the desired place. Am-
bition is strong, often so
dominating that it obscures
more worthy objectives. The
attraction is usually to a
business career--merchan-
dizing or building, contract-
ing or land transactions.
Whatever they undertake must
pay--even if the talent and
choice is directed to writ-
ing or (with a strong 5th
House) to the theatre. We
must realize that the ruler-
ship here is Saturn and that
the Saturn Card is the 10 S--
so success is practically
assured,

Ruler- Uranus.

To be satisfied, these
natives much deal with peop-
le--either by direct con-
tact or through work that
has a public appeal. Aquar-
ians are always free lances
and from a wide choice se-
lect the occupation that most
appeals to themselves-~as
long as it promises good re-
turns (8 D-- Uranus Card).
Writers, actors, clergymen,
statesmen or counselors and
group leaders can succeed.
Ruler- Neptune.

Here is a strong sense of
service and an urge to make
known the ideals to which
they are dedicated. There
is usually great attraction
for the sea and many are suc-
cessful in commerce, naval

affairs and foreign trade.
Good diagnosticians, dealers
in cosmetics and perfumes or
oil operators are found here--
also writers and philosophers.

April 6.Ruler- Mars.

Aries.

May 4.
Tau.

June 2.

Enthusiastic and impetuous,

but often beset with obstacles
and disappointments owing to
their tendency to choose the
easiest way. Subject to many
changes caused by circumstan-
ces. Make good writers, lectu-
rers, journalists--sometimes
actors or artists. Are able as
trial lawyers. Not sufficient-
ly patient or far-seeing to be-
come counselors or trustees.
Ruler- Venus.

Are public spirited and phil-
anthropic. Want peace and secu-
rity and strong home roots,
with luxurious surroundings.
Are successful in land deals,
horticulture and anything that
deals with natural products
and resources. Love of nature
is strong and they should live
in the country a part of the
year. Many poets and authors
are found in this date. If at-
tracted to public life, they
make good politicians and gov
ermment officials. In business,
can succeed as head of large
manufacturing concerns.

Ruler- Mercury.

Restless and active; always
have more than one iron in

the fire. Both social and bus-
iness contacts are essential;
must always have an audience.
Easy flow of words and make
good journalists, columnists
and correspondents. Many are
attracted to science (mainly
from curiosity) and the church
(mainly from their sense of
drama). They move quickly and
change frequently--in the
search for improvement. If
there is any monotony it comes
early in life.

THREE OF HEARTS

Hearts - Love

3H - Uncertainty in personal
relations.

3_in H - Happiness in contacts.

The Mercury Card in the Mercury L.
Displaces the A H in the Nat. Sp.

In the Mundane Spread we have
found that the 3 H is the "first
step out", Since the Mundane Spread
is a picture of our departure from
God's Plan, we may regard the 3 H
as the original parent of all the
mistakes--"departures"--that
follow, the Adam that symbolizes
the fall of man. We displaced the
desire for Love (A H) as the ru-
ler of our lives with a mental
uncertainty about love in general
and love of what or whom in par-
ticular. Perhaps it is the sub-
conscious realization of this
great error that so often makes
the love life of the 3 H an un-
satisfying-- or tragic-- thing,
and causes the eternal quest for
the perfect love-- and the doubt
of it when found.

As far as the emotions are con-
cerned, life for the 3 H is a se-
ries of trials and errors. Its
True Place (Natural Spread) is the
Mars Card in the Mercury Line, so
there is no lack of activity in
the quest. Their Fellow men never
give them a crown of fidelity but
it is not so much a question of
fickleness or promiscuity in their
case as an inner need for the one
love that satisfies the Self (A H).
The pity of it is that the criti-
eal faculty (Mercury) steps in and
sows the seeds of questioning and
doubt.

Socially, they are usually
charming and attractive people--

welcome guests and perfect hosts;
it is only in the closer relation-
ships that the strain becomes a
break.

They are always intelligent
and informed (Mercury Card in the
Mercury Line), but since their un-
certainty extends to their mental
processes they do not always dis-
tinguish clearly between right and
wrong, truth and falsehood-- unless
the early training has fixed the
distinction for them. They are of-
ten dominated in youth by the mo-
ther, later by the wife and there-
fore have the best chance for self-
development away from home. They
should never marry anyone who in-
terferes with their freedom-- even
in its uncertainty or misuse.

There are but two birthdates
ruled by this card, therefore but
two types of people to consider-
the Sagittarian (November 30) and
the Capricornian (December 28).

KKK KKK

Merc. Great interest (and curios-

Ac ity) regarding people. Eager

to discover and apply new

lines of thought. Should be
very particular to give cred-

it when the idea is not orig-
inal. Usually very talkative--
even verbose. Good story tell-
ers and good critics; never

at a loss for a word. Should
guard against prying into pri-
vate affairs-- and gossip.
Attracted to intelligent wom-
en but are not happy if mar-
ried to one of intellect super-
ior to their own. Married women
are apt to be interfered with
by their mothers-in-law or sis-
ters-in-law. Often form a valu-

able friendship with a wom-
an of spiritual insight and
intuitional gifts. Through
her they have an opportunity
to develop their own. Enjoy
social activities and like
to entertain groups of people
who are important in the pro-
fessional and literary world.
Success is indicated in any
line of activity seriously
undertaken, Work well with
friends, especially men. Are
depressed by an atmosphere of
inharmony, which interferes
with success. May become im-
portant in the business or
professional world. Can suc-
cessfully combine business
and social activities. Put
over deals at dinner parties;
transact business at the club,
etc. The women may become soc-
ial lights, leaders of salons,
etc.

Apt to change the vocation
of first choice. If finances
are limited or doubtful, they
keep changing occupations in
the hope of greater security.
Will always walk out if there
is stagnation or monotony--
but they usually walk into
uncertainty in that event.
There is often some burden
connected with home or the
emotional life that inter-
feres with accumulating an
income that is satisfactory.
Uncertainty may extend to
health-- of themselves or
others-- and interfere with
business and finances. Worry
over money is apt to cause
illness; distrust of the phy-
sician interferes with recov-
ery. Health insurance is a
Must for these people; other-
wise their surroundings in
illness may be very uncomfor-
table and the care they re-
ceive insufficient or unsat-
isfactory.

Uran.

Nep.

Sag.

Cap.

Nov.30.

Dec .28.

There is always a desire for
occult knowledge, but there
is likewise doubt and skepti-
cism about accepting it as
truth. It is only those who
are willing to make sacrifi-
ces for it who are able to
profit by it. May have psy-
chic gifts but hesitate to
use them. If not adherents
to strict honesty, can lead
“double lives" successfully.
Unless problems are over-~
come in the earlier years,
the end of life is not likely
to be happy or satisfactory.
Security must be built up be-
fore 50. They should have one
person in the life who will
remain faithful and devoted.
Travel proves disappointing
and does not help the rest-
lessness of the later years.
Their own devotion to an ob-
ject, a principle or an in-
dividual would go far toward
overcoming the difficulty.

Challenge for the 3H
LOYALTY

Birthdates Ruled by the 3 H

Ruler- Jupiter.

Good sportsmanship and pop-
ularity belong to this birth-
date. Clever with words-- but
seldom show their hand. Have
great influence with crowds;
understand mass psychology.
Good orators, writers, states-
men; often have inventive gifts.
Ruler- Saturn.

Have fits of stubborness but
are actually concerned about
their future. Fear insecurity.
Should avoid medicine as a ca-
reer; dislike physical con-
tacts. Interested in large en-
terprises; ambitious. May be-
come political leaders, states-
men. More faithful than Nov. 30.


## Page 51

-47-

THREE OF CLUBS

Clubs - Mental Attitudes
3C¢ - Uncertainty in beliefs.
3.in C- Ideas from Kindred Minds.

The Mars Card in the Saturn Line.
Displaces the 5 D in the Nat. Sp.

You will note that this card
carries a heavy burden of 3-- with
a strong emphasis on "heavy" since
it falls in the Saturn Line under
the emphatic influence of Mars.
Two 3's fall together-- the card
itself and its Mercury Card; its
True Place is in the Mars Line;
so a "Mars-Saturn Conjunction"
defines the undercurrent through-
out the life. Perhaps a slight
saving grace lies in the fact
that the True Place is in the
Venus position--but doubt about
the choice or stability of love-
relationships is likely to be as
disturbing as the shifting mental
attitudes. The cry for Peace seems
never to be answered for these
people until they learn to depend
solely upon themselves and their
inner resources.

The displacement of the 5 D
bespeaks money as a major factor
in uncertainty. The periods of
steady and dependable income are
few and far between. There is
often a change-- or several chan-
ges- in occupation in the hope of
finding means of increasing the
income.

Despite the shifts in view-
point, there is seldom a desire
to change themselves- their own
established concepts and intoler-
ance of the new and untried; it
is partly the inability to decide
on the right course, partly stub-
bornness. All Clubs feel that their
mental attitudes are right. They
do have an inner knowledge-- but
they don't always use it.

Usually willing to acknowledge
their mistakes and willing to try
again-~- but with no confidence in
the new effort; mentally, they are
beaten before they start.

The more developed ones-- those
who are aware of their intuitive
gifts and of their inheritance of
knowledge-- will invariably turn to
metaphysics for their solution--
and will find it. Their security
then becomes dependable and they
abandon the role of "Doubting Thom-
ases",

There may be some misfortune
connected with death and inherit-
ance; something way interfere with
receiving their rights, payment of
debts owned them or money that is
legally their own. There is also
some danger of accident in these
birthdates-- Mars-Saturn being a
combination to watch, and uncer-
tainty of direction being a menance
at all times.

Decisions should be made care-
fully and slowly-- then believed
in and held to. They should be will-
ing to abandon tradition in this
changing world and to accept new
values in the name of growth. They
should strive, through meditation
and the cultivation of their own
spiritual power, to work with what
the soul knows from past experience,
not against it.
Planetary Sequence for the 3 C

Merc. (Note the two 3's together).

38 A sense of insecurity may
last until the 28th year.
Always two patterns to pur-
sue, two paths to choose
from. May have two occupa-
tions at the same time. Many
short trips. Any business
will require money and ef-
fort.

Birthdates Ruled by the 3 C

May 29,
Gem.

June 27.
Can.

July 25.
leo.

Ruler- Mercury.

Highstrung, restless and
nervous. Constantly on the go.
Have at least two irons in the
fire at a time. Should culti-
vate a hobby or sideline that
holds their interest. Are ad-
aptable and versatile, but not
good stickers unless interest-
ed in a cause or an individual.
Well suited to public life--
stage, politics, lecturing.
Clever and good investigators--
but not researchers. Good at
salesmanship if allowed to
travel; should never be tied

to a desk or a boring occupa-
tion. Skilful with their hands.
Ruler- The Moon.

Can deal successfully with
children. The women make good
nurses, devoted and motherly.
Home is their center. Will take
many responsibilities of others
on their own shoulders. Willing
to sacrifice for loved ones.
Like to be before the public or
be considered the center of some
branch of public life. Have a
strong sense of drama and appre-
ciation of music. Can succeed at
teaching, direction, dressmaking,
millinery.

Ruler- The Sun

Have more power and strength
than the other 3 C-- and are
aware of it. A law unto them-
selves, not usually orthodox.
Dictatorial in own line of work.
Best of all professions for
them is the theatre-- but not ne-
cessarily acting. Make good di-
rectors and producers. May at-
tain a high place if willing to
work hard and stick to their de-
cisions. Work may be interfered
with through ill health. Good
executors, statesmen, leaders.
Fundamentally spiritual, but
not always considered so. Can
commercialize art.

Aug.23. Ruler- Sun or Mercury.
Leo-Vir.Want power but prefer to

Sept.21.
Vir.

Oct.19.
Lib.

leave responsibility to
others. If in the army will al-
ways "'pass the buck''. If Leo
predominates, may be perform-
ers-- actors, musicians, etc.
If Virgo, good scientists-- es-
pecially chemists. Can be very
calculating. Can succeed in
banking, real estate or as pro-
fessors and teachers of adults.
Investigating turn of mind; of-
ten have wanderlust-- from men-
tal curiosity. Subject to ner-
vous indigestion and should be
careful of diet. Good in the
publishing field, preferring
educational books. Many are
successful writers,

Ruler- Mercury.

Sensitive and nervous. Dis-
satisfied with own accomp-
lishment. Need praise and ap-
proval. Have keen minds and
high ideals. Should guard a-
gainst depression and discour-
agement. Long for success and
try many ways of attaining it--
not fully trusting any of them.
Inclined to belittle their own
abilities. Great readers and
investigators. The most spir-
itually-minded of the 3 C.
Choice and discriminating in
taste. Writers, publishers, in-
vestigators. More concerned
with the interests of others
than their own. Often talent-
ed in art but cannot commer-
cialize it. Lack self-assurance
Ruler- Venus.

Independent; inclined to
self-indulgence. Should guard
against selfishness. Origin-
al in thought. Life often dis-
turbed by outside interference.
Can commercialize art. Success-
ful at law, music, plastics.
Writers,-- sometimes poets.
Want harmony and like to please
but not given to sacrifice un-
less obliged to.

Planetary Sequence for the 3 D

Merc.
AS

~
=

Mars.

There is a keen desire for
Truth, but it is not always
sought beyond the limits of
expediency. The less develop-
ed ones become crafty and se-
cretive, unwilling to display
their hand and lose some fan-
cied advantage. Often feel
that the end justifies the
means. Those who are aware of
their destiny become great ex-
ponents and teachers of meta-
physics, Among them there is
full realization that they
are but agents and trustees
of whatever gifts they have
and that their minds must be
kept unceasingly on the high-
er levels in order to receive
the direction and inspiration
that will not fail them. They
are eager to give forth their
knowledge for the benefit of
others.

May become victims of unre-
liable friends or associates.
If they have beauty, material
security or unusual advantages
are subject to jealousy and
gossip. Apt to make a marriage
that is disappointing. Should
be wary of giving confidence
or releasing own rights; may
have trouble in recovering
them. Because of affectional
disappointment are often driv-
en back upon themselves that
they may re-discover their own
power and self-sufficiency.
Partnerships or other close
associations with men not
usually successful. In the
case of women, if there is
compatibility, the happiness
may not last. Husband, son or
brother may be taken by death
or a separation may be forced.
If not compatible, men may
cause trouble in finances,
unreasonable demands or dom-
ination.

Changes in occupation-~ ei-
ther forced or voluntary. If
they adhere to the same type
of business, will change the
method or approach, Business
often benefitted by travel.
Should seek business associ-
ates among powerful and in-

and friendliness essential to

Should not remain too long in
one place.

Note that this is one of the
fixed cards-- always found in
the same position and always
the same as the card it dis-
places. Here being the J H
under Saturn, the element of
sacrifice is emphasized-- u-
sually because of some forced
limitation or through the ill-
ness of some one toward whom
there is an obligation--real
or fancied. May become a mar-
tyr to duty. These people
have healing power and can ac-
complish great good through it.
which discourages and blocks
them. Should analyze causes
and refuse to be influenced by
others. Not well adapted to
dealings with labor groups or
likely to have loyalty from
employees. Unless highly de-
veloped and sure of their
ground, should avoid psychism.
Contact with the spirit world
is apt to be disappointing and
unreliable. If spiritually en-
lightened, can receive direct
illumination and sure guidance.
Mundanely, 9 is disappoint-
ment and loss; spiritually it
is fulfilment. If the mental
attitudes (A S) have been
rightly directed, peace will
come in the later years. Mat-
ters at a distance are not
favored; travel (after 50) is
disappointing. Should not live
near the sea.

-53-

July 12.Ruler- The Moon.

Can. Fear insecurity. Very de-
pendent upon others; want
comfort and cannot always
earn enough to assure it. Do
not take kindly to interfer-
ence, but will sacrifice for
loved ones. Demand a home but
dislike any limitation in it.
Dominated by a desire for love
but are often disappointed.
Given more to philosophy and
theories derived from tradi-
tion and past experience than
to progress and changes. Are
useful in a public capacity--
as politicians, welfare work-
ers, reformers (according to
orthodox rules). Like a posi-
tion of prominence but need
support from others,

Aug. 10.Ruler- The Sun.

Leo Are natural leaders and pro-
moters but have a sense of is-
olation when they become prom-
inent. Love deeply and are loy-
al; when the idol is broken,
have no desire to rebuild. Too
sensitive for their own good.
Public-spirited; able and suc-
cessful in public life. Self-
protective because uncertain
of the future. Succeed best
as a head of own business. Are
dynamic writers, good propa-
gandists. Can succeed in mer-
chandizing and manufacturing.
Are dramatic and effective.

Sept. 8.Ruler- Mercury.

Vir. More material-minded and
less aware of their true des-
tiny than many other 3 D. Apt
to be swamped with detail and
have a narrow viewpoint. Can
become penurious if they are
not watchful. Analytical and
meticulous. Neglect no small
points but often lose the lar-
ger vision, Can succeed as
public servants, writers or
lawyers (corporation, not tri-
al). Good researchers. Want
practical results and good re-
turn for their efforts.

Oct. 6. Ruler- Venus

Lib.

Nov. 4.

Scor.

Dec.
Sag.

2.

Want peace and easy con-
ditions, but uncertainty in-
terferes with contentment.
More protected than many 3 D
but always fear the poorhouse.
Are intuitive and find many
"answers" -- then doubt them.
Attracted to the limelight
and can become good actors,
playwrights or lecturers.
Good hosts and entertainers.
Love the country and even go
in for sports to keep them

in the open-- although bet-
ter adapted for an artistic
or literary career. Very va-
cillating in opinions and in-
capable of firm decisions.
Ruler- Mars,

Like all 3's, have doubts

and indecision but give the
impression of being very set
and sure of themselves. Suf-
fer through love but remain
loyal and continue to sacri-
fice. Keep their troubles to
themselves. Have a keen under-
standing of human foibles and
an over-ready philosophy to
apply to them, Often attract-
ed to drugs or medicine and
ean succeed in all branches
of healing. Keen searchers
for truth-- and causes. Out-
wardly critical. Good at man-
ual arts-- sculpture, model-
ing in clay, etc.

Ruler- Jupiter.

Want success and will make
frequent changes to obtain it.
Need congenial ‘surroundings
and harmony in associations.
Sensitive and magnetic-- of-
ten very aware spiritually.
Must never deviate from their
ideals or will end in failure.
Inwardly know the Law, but
fear it-- and fear not to fol-
low it. Meet many disappoint-
ments and frustrations. Often
put in a position that is for-
eign to their nature or beyond
their ability. Good writers.

Planetary Sequence for the 3 S

q
fo}

Subject to disappointment

in people-- usually as the

result of poor judgment. If

they get into trouble, must

work it out for themselves.

Seldom get help from others.

Should never gamble; the poor

judgment extends to finances.

(See the displaced 7 D).

Must never incur debts they

hope to be able to pay; the

money must be in the bank or

there must be security given.

Home life may be unsatisfac-

tory because of limited fi-

nances. Instead of choosing

carefully friends who are

trustworthy, are usually

skeptical about all friend- Uran.
ships. May meet opposition 9D
in efforts to raise money.
Are swayed by gossip or may
become victims of it if the
life is not above reproach.
Business competitors bring
changes and shifts of poji-
cy, causing fluctuation in
income and failure to become
established. May be interest-
ed in distant transactions,
acting as brokers or agents.
Often cause their own finan-
cial burdens by refusing to
follow advice or becoming
set in their own opinions.
Apt to act on impulse and
then make changes to cover
up the mistake.

If associated with a hard-
working woman can be con~
siderably helped. Should see
that employees are reliable.
If a physician, should seek
help from a woman nurse or
doctor. In any line, a woman
manager is advisable; she
will help to mitigate any
loss. Best to hire women ser-
vants or business associates
whenever possible. Will often
make money through them.

off
n

Note that there are 2 Jacks
here; the card that is dis-
placed is the J D. Positive-
ly, Jacks are valuable and
important; negatively, they
are sly, crafty, frivolous
and irresponsible. Under the
disciplinary Saturn, this is
a warning to live strictly
and soberly-~ no drinking or
later hours; no self-indul-
gence that interferes with
work or duty. Obligations
may be increased by some mem-
ber of the family-- father,
brother or son who is a prob-
lem, an expense, is afflict-
ed or in poor health. This
card in this position should
be regarded as a challenge.
If investing in real estate
should avoid anything that
is speculative in nature or
that promises a quick turn-
over in a re-sale, Invest-
ments of any kind should be
for a long term. Should keep
out of any difficulty that
involves labor groups or
trade unions. Should never
be involved in their dis-
putes or try to uphold their
rights. May have trouble
with employees. If employed,
may not be adequately paid.
Travel will not be satis~
factory or reminerative.
Should not live near the
water; if there is a tenden-
cy to colds, rheumatism, etc.
it will be aggravated. Best
to avoid any occupation con-
nected with shipping, li-
quids or medicines; perfume
or oil.

## Page 61

-57-

4 FOURS 4

OURS represent Enclosure,

Completion, FOUNDATION. The

pattern is the square--or the

solid square, the cube. 4 is
our Fenced Field, our Security--
and therefore our Protection.

"Sentinels" are at the 4 cor-
ners of the field, assuring our
safety within it; the field it-
self is ours-- to build in.

4 is the symbol for Earth,
the 4th "element". We "fell" into
"matter" that we might work our
way out of it, so we know that
despite the security and protec-
tion that surrounds us, there is
to be no idleness within the God-
given enclosure that is 4. We are
to build a firm and unassailable
foundation (4); we are to labor
(4) with concentration (4) and
diligence (4) and secure (4) for
ourselves the right to work out
our pattern in freedom from un-
conquerable obstacles, poverty,
heartache and failure. We must
bear in mind that 4 is the num-
ber of Saturn, and that he hands
out the rewards if and when they
are earned-- and only so.

As Birth Cards, 4's are among
the most fortunate. They give us
a wonderful start-- with protect-
ion, security, sufficiency-- but
like every other card and every
birth pattern, the course of our
lives and their finish is up to
us. Of the 4 spots or "sentinels"
two are matter and two are spirit;
in 4 they are united. He who at-
tempts to separate them builds
his foundation on sand and the
wind and floods sweep it from
under him. He finds himself in
an empty field-- save for Saturn.

The 4th Sphere on the Tree of
Life is Chesed-- Mercy-- the realm
of Jupiter. The 4th Statement in
the Pattern on the Trestleboard is
"From the Limitless Substance I
draw all things needful, both
spiritual and material".

To the Pythagoreans 4 was the
Sacred Number, for its elements--
1, 2, 3 and 4 when summed up are
equal to 10 "which is so perfect
that we can go no further, but to
increase we must return to the
Monad", (Wynn Westcott).

For our 4's, then, the prime
admonition is to BUILD.

HEARTS are to build their secu-
rity on love for their
fellow man if they may
hope for love in their
own lives.

CLUBS are to build on Knowledge-
to be shared and dissemin-
ated for the profit, edu-
cation and growth of all.

DIAMONDS are to build on VALUES
that are everlasting.

SPADES are to labor, with hands
and hearts and minds for
the WISDOM that is of God,
That is their foundation
and security. Their miss-
ion is to shed the Light
they have found on every
dark corner, on all blind
eyes and every burdened
heart.

As in the Tarot, the 4 is
an Emperor. 4's have come to be
and can be in command of every
situation that arises. Their task
is organization. They are dealing
with practicalitiés-- and they
have the power to glorify them.

oh E

t, Sequence for the 4 H

=59-

cE
ic
is)

Want financial security and
work for freedom in the use

of money early in life. Are
interested in quick turnovers
and speedy returns from any
investment. The ability to ac-
cumulate money through their
own efforts gives them great
satisfaction. There is usual-
ly a good financial background
to work from and rarely any
actual lack in their early en-
vironment. They are inclined
to be practical and level-
headed when it comes to expen-
ditures for education or any
necessary equipment. Sat.
Strong home ties and depend- 6S
ence on cooperation. They
dislike changes of home and

in family relationships. Hos-
pitable and socially inclined.
They like to surround them-
selves with congenial groups
and prefer their own homes as
a meeting place. In intimate
associations they are attract-
ed to people of good standing
but will not exclude those of
limited means if they have oth-
er assets that meet their stan-
dards. Like to join art, edu-
cational or cultural classes.
Fond of entertainment~- usu-
ally high class. Good enter-
tainers themselves and cordial
hosts. Are inclined to spend Uran.
considerable time in dancing, QH
theatre-going and general ex-
citement -- and later have a
sense of regret over the waste
of effort and the lack of ful-
filment derived. They want
amusement and diversion but

do not want to sacrifice any
of their power through the ill
affects of self-indulgence.
Good sports and willing to pay
for their fun-- but are not
pleased with themselves when
anything is neglected.

Benefit by following their
intuitions-- which are re~
liable, There is a definite
cleavage between the positive
and negative aspects of this
position. For the positives,
harmony and security are as-
sured by diligently working
for it-- "keeping the wheels
greased". The negatives are
likely to fall into a rut be-
cause of laziness and self-
satisfaction. If sufficiently
provided for they find it eas-
ier to rest on their oars and
be content with less than to
bestir themselves and achieve
a better situation.

These people have a founda~
tion of good health but may
injure it by self-indulgence
or by involving themselves
with personalities that are
undesirable or unsatisfactory.
The consequence is worry that
disturbs the health and may
set up a chronic condition
that is hard to overcome. The
conflict usually comes from
operating under the Person-
ality Card rather than the
Birth Card-- especially in
the case of women. 4 H has
an innate knowledge of Divine
Law and should not deviate
from it. Are attracted to the
drugless field and are natur-
al healers.

When used constructively,
intuition and inspiration
are strong in this card. If
problems are to be met or im-
portant decisions to be made,
serious reflection and medi-
tation will produce a safe
guide, Mistakes in invest-
ments-- especially real est-
ate-- are rarely made; deal-
ings with groups and organi-
zations are profitable and
successful; employees are co-
operative and faithful. En-
lightenment is assured.

## Page 65

-61-

These people make good prop~
agandists in the lines in which
they are interested, The judgment
is usually sound and the appeal
is to those of intelligence and
common sense, There is a tendency
to cling to tradition and princi-
ple, but not to the extent that
interferes with progress. This is
one of the Patriot cards inasmuch
as there is no departure from
fundamentals, They will fight for
their interpretation of the law
if they believe it is a good law
to start with.

Between the men and women of
this card there is a basic equal-
ity. The Queen of Clubs is as pow-
erful in her way as either the
King or the Jack; her judgment is
usually as sound and her intui-
tion superior. Then, too, she oc~
cupies the central position in
the Natural Spread and in this
age of intuition and extra-sen-
sory perception, she is given her
place of equality. In the realm
of politics and political econo-
my she is, in many instances, u-
surping the place formerly held
exclusively by men and it is her
job, as the 4 C, to prove that
she can hold it-- and perhaps im-
prove upon it. The Jupiter posi-
tion bespeaks his blessing on this
situation because it is evolution-
ary. The keynote for this man-
woman combination is Cooperation.
Together they will gain more wis-
dom than would be possible alone.

The keen intelligence of this
Mars-Jupiter conjunction makes
these people intolerant of stupid-
ity and triviality for they are
fundamentally mental (Clubs) and
they realize that growth and ex-
pansion (Jupiter) are possible on-
ly through constant activity (Mars)
along mental lines (C).

The undeveloped ones are apt
to talk much and say little. Their

right to the 4 C as a Birth Card
gives them a hearing, but unless
they have learned to clarify and
organize their ideas they will
not hold their audience.

These are the arguers and de-
baters-- the lawyers with volum-
inous briefs, the speakers with
lengthy paragraphs, the writers
whose introductions are longer
than the subject matter, Unless
they are lazy and careless-- which
is rare-- they are concerned on-
ly with matters of importance.
they are seldom willing to waste
their time or brains on inconse-
quentials.

They are good travelers and
interesting companions-- always
ready to point out something that
everybody else has missed. They
are, of necessity, usually at-
tracted to professions and ment-
al pursuits-- teaching, lectur-
ing, philosophy, education, pol-
itics and economics, If in busi-
ness, they want their indepen-
dence and an opportunity to pro-
ject their own ideas. Only in
rare cases are the women domes-
tically inclined; their best ex-
pression is in an independent
business or in the literary or
educational field.

Planet Sequence for the 4 C.

Merc. Money is of early impor-

2D tance, for it represents
an avenue of freedom. While
still young they learn to bar-
gain. Business propositions
come suddenly and unexpected-
ly; travel and changes without
warning. If circumstances re-
quire it, they change their
opinions readily but usually
maintain a good mental bal-
ance, When they are certain
of their knowledge they can-
not be talked out of a stand
taken, Good soap box orators.

May 28.

June 26,

July 24.
Leo.

Aug. 22.
Leo-Vir.

-63-

Ruler- Mercury.

Good agents and go-be~
tweens. Keen, inquiring
minds. Must have occupation
that moves fast. Should av-
oid medicine as a career ex-
cept as mental or nerve spe-
cialists. Good talkers, lec-
turers. Interested in law,
diplomacy or the market, Can
succeed as engineers or sci-
entists, Should guard against
superficiality, procrastina-
tion. Apt to scatter the for-
ces. Work best with others.
Ruler- The Moon
Self-indulgent; usually

put on much weight. Must
take good care of teeth; may
tend to crumble. Natural a-
bility for dealing with oth-
ers. Often talented-- in
singing or working in metal
or clay. Successful in work
with the ground-- raising
commodities, growing flow-
ers, profiting by oil. May
become food experts, diet-
icians, prize chefs. May
have talent for the theatre.
Ruler- The Sun.

Responsible leaders. Want
public life or prominence.
Dramatic, spectacular. Act-
ors, dramatists. Want to dis-
cover or initiate something
of importance. May become
public philanthropists, wel-
fare promoters, art sponsors.
Charitable-- but want their
gifts publicized.

Rulers-- The Sun or Merc.
Less spectacular than

July 24, often better bal-
anced, but equally gifted.
May become outstanding in
dramatic or musical field.
May devote their lives to a
cause; have strong opinions
and beliefs. Sensitive, but
practical, Love the country,
children and dogs. Idealists
but remain practical, Excel-
lent parents.

Sept.20.Ruler-Mercury.

Vir.

Oct.
Lib.

Have intuition and inspi-
ration-- but fight them;
want to remain practical.
Often choose the easiest way
through laziness or expedi-
ency. If remain true to the
best of themselves, can ac~
complish much. May be drawn
to law, counseling, psych-
ology, research-- especially
of disease. Want personal
freedom. Should choose an
occupation that is mental.
If tied to home, should have
a hobby.

18.Ruler- Venus.

Friendly, popular. Busi-
ness interests advanced

by personality. Can become
a power in groups. Like to
shine -- as socialites, en-
tertainers, artists. Usually
well groomed. Women succeed
as stylists, models, beauti-
cians. Work best if married
or in partnership. May meet
opposition from family. Can
succeed as lawyers or poli-
ticians.

Nov. 16.Ruler- Mars.

Scor.

Set and fixed in ideas,

Want to promote what they
believe in. Will espouse cau-
ses; public spirited. Intense
and dramatic; usually have mu-
sical talent. Not always suc-
cessful in marriage; have i-
deals and want others to live
up to them. Good government
officials, statesmen. Have a
long-range vision. Men (espe-
cially) should guard against
self-indulgence.

Dec. 14.Ruler- Jupiter.

Born speculators, but of-

ten bound to a routine oc-
cupation. A karmic date; have
come to settle obligations.
Honest, but reckless; care-
less of consequences. Nervous
and tense. Can write, lecture,
sell- but only if interested.
Philosophical in later years.

Some sort of work is usu-
ally undertaken early in

life. Associations necessary};
there is an early fear of be-
ing left with responsibility
and decisions. Much involved
with agreements, messages,
communications, letters and
telephone calls. May engage
in work associated with these
things. Always want things
definite and clarified-- set
down on paper. Except for the
birthdates under the mental
signs, are not especially in-
terested in education.

May form a platonic friend-
ship that lasts a long time.
Are not eager for the respon-
sibility of marriage-- but
may marry for protection and
security. May make many friends
in some group activity-- often
religious, Marriage not always
satisfactory; some unforeseen
obstacle often arises that cau-
ses disappointment, but if a
break occurs, it is usually
brought about by the other
partner.

Want peace and harmonious
conditions. Eager for suf-
ficient knowledge to bring a-
bout improvement. Feel that
it can be found in experience
rather than in books. If con-
tacts are congenial and condi-
tions fairly smooth, may get
into a rut and stay there.
Will have progress if they
make an effort.

If in a commercial occupa-
tion they are likely to
remain there. If spiritually
developed, can become mental
healers. Can have good, steady
income if are diligent and con-
centrated in work and do not
seek unreasonable expansion.
If meney dominates, their nat-
ural protection is lost and

2a

Uran.

fo)
i}

P|

business difficulties arise.
Subject to disappointment in
work-associates-- usually
from failure to assume their
own share of responsibility.
The 6 S is one of the "ini-
tiate"” cards. The enlighten-
ed 4 D native will apply met-
aphysics to his business.

The mother, wife or some
female relative may pres-~
ent a problem or become a
means of expense. There is
indicated here a karmic at-
tachment-- possibly a debt--
to be discharged. For these
people themselves, health
may be a problem, but they
are usually well taken care
of. There may be marriage

to an older woman (in the
case of the men) and she may
prove to be a hindrance. If
a woman, marriage is desired
but is not always a means to
happiness.

Find contentment in deal-
ing in real estate, prod-
ucts of the earth, building,
etc. Should ally themselves
with progressive and humani-
tarian groups, fraternities,
etc, Can become outstanding
leaders. Such a powerful card
under Uranus indicates a val-
uable intuitional gift. If
this is cultivated, can de-
pend upon guidance. Unless
wholly self-centered, will
be divinely directed to chan-
nels of success,

The latter years are apt

to be more financially pro-
tected than the earlier. May
have a legacy or substantial
inheritance-- although prob-
ably not without some confu-
sion attached to it, These
people should have no desire
to retire from business until
far advanced in years. Will
be happier and more useful if
they remain active. May travel.

## Page 71

July 11.
Can.

Aug. 9.
Leo.
Sept. 7.
Vir.

-67-

Ruler- The Moon.

Very emotional, self-con-
cerned. When they forget
themselves, become success-
ful in business, useful in
the community. Concerned with
homes, families, housing, etc.
Can deal in commodities-- what
the public needs and wants,
Paternal (or maternal) and
protective. Like to shine as
public benefactors. Nervous
and restless; never feel they
are fully appreciated. Have
a sense of service but are
often too lazy to let it man-
ifest. Want comfort with-

out effort,

Ruler- The Sun,

Very keen for success. Do
well with business if al-
ready established-- but want
it on a large scale. Always
want value received. Are ei-
ther self-centered or just
the opposite-- humanitarian
and self-sacrificing. May be
attracted to religious groups;
if the self-seeking type, can
make the connection pay. Are
good organizers. Can succeed
as actors but an equal num-
ber do just as well as mer-
chants and manufacturers.

Are sympathetic-- sometimes
patronizing.

Ruler- Mercury.

Inclined to science and
research. Should follow a
line that requires good judg-
ment and a keen mind. May be
fussy and meticulous if not
careful-- also petty in per-
sonal relationships. Sharp
and clever-- sometimes too
much so, If religiously in-
clined, want demonstrations.
CAN be very high-minded.

Good writers, teachers, edu-
cators; often have keen sense
of humor. Shculd avoid work-
ing for expediency rather
than mutual benefit.

Oct. 5.
Lib.

Nov. 3.
Scor,

Dec. 1.
Sag.

Ruler- Venus.

Performers, artists, wri-
ters. Much attracted to

the stage or screen. Want

to be a power in their own
circle, Make good lawyers,
politicians, leaders. Good
agents and go-betweens, Are
friendly and co-operative.
Have strong metaphysical in-
clinations. Emotional and
self-indulgent; if overcome
those traits, can develop
much soul-force. Always have
an eye for beauty; always
present a good appearance.
Need many contacts and chan-
ges to keep interest alive.
Ruler- Mars.

Much financial power in

this birthdate, but many
prefer the easiest way and
will not make the necessary
effort, Should avoid getting
into a rut. Can gain much
hidden knowledge if they seek
for it. Fixed and set in their
thinking; hard to convince.
Have inner fear of lack of
money, but do little to fore-
stall it. Can succeed in "big"
business-- especially manu-
facturing. Have a gift for
writing, but must cultivate
it. Many of the deeper think-
ers become poets and compos-~
ers.

Ruler- Jupiter.

Some woman may be very in-
fluential in this life.
Dependent upon close associa-
tions and will take responsi-
bility for them. Nervous a-
bout making changes, so apt
to remain in one place for a
long time. Want fréedom and
independence in finances and
willing to work hard to keep
it. Good for travel business,
foreign connections, law or
diplomacy. Good foreign cor-
respondents. Can become able
and popular leaders.

Friendly contacts in early
life. Usually brought up

in a family that is kindly and
affectionate, Dependent upon
congenial and understanding
teachers for best progress in
schools Like to associate with
those of kindred minds and in-
terests. Cultivation of con-
tacts a big factor in future
success. This card is better
for a man than a woman in the
early years; the women are apt
to become too dependent emo-
tionally,

Naturally gravitate toward
those who have money or good
background. May give too much
importance to prominence and
social standing. Are attracted
to art and want to accomplish
something in an artistic line--
but only if it can be made to
pay. If not, it is soon aban-
doned. Usually ambitious to
make a good marriage--as much
for prestige as for security.
Want beauty in their surround-
ings. Should strive to look
beyond appearances for values.
The original displacement

of the 10 C indicates suc-
cess in any line diligently
pursued; the 8 S under Mars
confirms it. They prefer work
in organizations where men pre-
dominate and want any business
they are connected with to be
capable of expansion. The men

, work well with groups and are

attracted to clubs.

There is a strong desire for
money-- for entertaining and
display, but also for charity.
These people are natural phil-
anthropists and make large con-
tributions to causes in which
they believe. They want every-
body to be comfortable and at
peace; they believe that sup-
ply is adequate for the entire

ic
It
lo
is

2
i=}

world, if properly distrib-
uted. Should cultivate the
habit of "not letting the

left hand know what the right
hand gives". Are too apt to
want their names attached to
their gifts.

May fail to reach their ob-
jectives through such a

strong desire for money that
worry interferes with their
accomplishment. They know bet-
ter, but there is always a
fear of lack. Should cultivate
a keener sense of values and
realize that work and self-
discipline will bring their

own rewards. Can succeed (and
profit) in work along healing
lines, Make good consultants
and diagnosticians. Can al-
ways overcome their difficul-
ties and are always protected.
Some woman of strong per-
sonality or psychic power

may have a marked influence on
their lives. In business, should
have a good business woman for
keeping accounts and directing
expenditures, Such a one is es-
pecially valuable in any work
along unusual or original lines,
Should not adhere too closely
to traditional methods, Can suc-
ceed-- often brilliantly-- in
untried fields, especially if
the results would be of univer-
sal benefit. Any inventive a-
bility should be cultivated.
Especially in later years,
money will be spent for trav-
el- usually with satisfactory
results. The changes that come
are apt to be beneficial and
agreeable, After 45 the occupa-
tion itself may have radical
changes. These should not be
resisted as they usually work
out to advantage. At all times
during the life these people
must follow the line of work
they like and for which they
feel best adapted,

## Page 75

-71-

5 FIVES 5

IVES represent Changes, Vari-

ety, Opportunity, Travel, Es-
cape and fluctuating Life Experi-
ence.

Look carefully at the forma-

tion of the spots and you will
see that 5 is a Cross. This is
logical enough when we reflect
that 5 is the Number of Man and
his (original) 5 senses.

Life experience is of necess-
ity a cross. Changes and surprises
we regard with disfavor since it is
but human to fear the unfamiliar
or unknown. We may regard
5 solely in this light if we
choose to-- but the wise ones re-
cognize Change as Growth, the re-
lease from the well-worn rut as
Opportunity.

Whatever our point of view,
the 5 natives are restless--and
usually dissatisfied. They want
change because they do not want
what they have, but as soon as
the change is made--still fear-
ful of what lies ahead--they
want to change the change. There
is always the chance that more
freedom lies ahead--and Freedom
is their battle-cry.

It is difficult for these peo-
ple to concentrate. They stand in
the center and strive to reach all
corners at the same time. They are
much like the mythical knight of
old who mounted his horse and rode
off in all directions. Always seek-
ing new places and new faces, new
occupations and new loves, new ex-
periences and new changes.

This is by no means the whole
story of 5. While the choice is
for experience rather than achieve-

ment, 5 gains great understanding
of his fellow man; he is strict-
ly honest and strictly just (un-
less operating wholly negatively)
for his 6th sense tells him that
only thus may he expect honesty

and justice from others. He un-
derstands the 5 steps of progres-
sion in the scheme of creation--
stone, plant, animal, man, God--
and he feels, if he seeks far e-
nough and keeps moving and obser-
ving, he will reach the topmost.

The discontent is not always
"divine"; it easily descends to
chronic disaffection with people,
surroundings and life in general,
Abhorring routine, disclaiming
responsibility, fearful of any
inroad on their personal freedom,
they are not always dependable
or faithful; their sense of jus-
tice does not extend to ties
that could-= and perhaps should--
bind them. Their own growth is
vital but they should realize
that it is not a very laudable
type of growth when it is achiev-
ed at the expense of those toward
whom they have obligations.

HEARTS have the problem of unsat-
isfied emotions.

CLUBS of a chronic mental rest-
lessness-- and no peace.

DIAMONDS of money that is never
enough.

SPADES of ill-paid labor,

5's mist realize the differ-
ence between good and bad rest-
lessness. Changes imposed from
without, in accordance with evo-
lutionary law carry us up the spi-
ral. Voluntary changes from a
sense of discontent deprive us of
our right to final peace.

Planetary Sequence for the 5 H

a

3¢

eo
io

we
nw

9H

Confusion and indecision

rule the early years of

life. Schooling is often in-
terfered with, either through
forced changes or limited fam-
ily finances. They are undeci- Jup.
ded about a career and no soon- 7 C
er do they prepare for one

than they shift to another.
They are always seeking oppor-
tunities to make money for
themselves-- mainly because
dependence upon others keeps
them tied to home and family.
There may be many occasions
for travel, but the money prob-
lem interferes with their en-
joyment.

There is a rather imperson-

al and detached feeling

toward family and close kin.

In romance much indecision

and fluctuation. These are Sat.
the people who are given to 5D

summer attachments and vaca-
tion crushes-- but a change of
scene usually brings a change
of mind and they decide that
the new love is not the right
one. If actually committed,
many will go through with the
bargain but will soon begin to
look around for means of es-
cape. It is difficult for
them to form roots; when they
do they regard them as chains
or ruts and are often made ill
by a sense of monotony.
Dealings with men are sel-
dom satisfactory-- for ei- Qs
ther sex. These natives are

"lone wolves" and while there

is much curiosity about people

and an eagerness to make new
contacts, dealings with them

are seldom satisfactory and

they want to pass on quickly

to others. Obstacles arise

from which they want to escape

or they become disappointed in

the people themselves-- and

leave. There is a streak

of laziness in many and they
will not take the trouble to
work out their problems. If
they do they invariably have
the reward of overcoming and
can proceed to success.

All business dealing must
be carried out in strict
honesty. It is easy for
these people to exaggerate
or distort. They are often
saddled with partners or as
sociates who fail to carry
their share of the load; sub-
ject to trickery and deceit
on the part of others and
must be careful to have all
transactions fully under-
stood and recorded. Are not
well favored in legal mat-
ters and in case of dispute
should always try to settle
out of court.

Health may be a problem
unless well fortified in
youth. Money is spent for
care and remedies that never
seem satisfactory or the
health of some member of the
family may interfere with
business and be costly. This
is a situation where change
is advisable for health is
often benefitted by getting
away from home. Apt to make
many changes in doctors and
nurses. Often increase their
ailments by trying too many
remedies and "cures".

If associated with groups

or fraternities, want to
run things and introduce va-
rious systems and unusual i-
deas. Are often benefitted
by association with a hard-
working, practical woman who
is capable of assuming res-
ponsibility. Such an associa-
tion may turn out to be a
life saver financially. With
good advice, can often make
money in real estate.

## Page 79

FIVE OF CLUBS

Clubs - Knowledge
5 Cc - Mental Curiosity
5_in C - Changes in Mental Atti-

tudes.
The Saturn Card in the Mercury L
Displaces the 5 H in the Nat. Sp.

There is a close tie-up with
the 5 H (by Displacement) and we
may expect to find many similar
problems, Since the 5 C is less
dependent upon affection than the
5 H, the difficulties will be less
of the heart than of the mind.
Nevertheless, there is emotional
imbalance and a sense of insecu-
rity in relationships.

By rulership, although Saturn
is most strongly emphasized in the
mental reactions, the True Place
offers a measure of protection by
its Jupiter position in the Mars
Line. In the 5 H this is lacking.

The 5 C is a young soul at
cross purposes with itself. Rest-
less, inquiring, seeking, these
natives are never satisfied with
the "answers" they find in life-
experience, They are constantly
meeting with obstacles and never
know quite what to do with them.
They want constant movement and
wide travel-- eager to go anywhere
rather than remain where they are.
The mistake they make is dashing
off on impulse, refusing to plan
in advance or count the cost. If
they would but engrave on their
minds the familiar railroad sign
of the country crossroads--"Stop,
Look and Listen''-- they would come
closer to peace of mind.

They have the equipment for
acquiring a rounded-out knowledge;
they have the natural inclination
toward a sound edutation but they
usually lack the faculty for apply-

ing what they learn, having a
conviction that all that is gen-
eral and usual and useful does

not apply in their case. The

sense of ego is strong; they feel
themselves to be special people,
especially singled out for trouble.

The brilliant exceptions are
those who educate themselves in
some specialty that interests them
and then pursue it to a successful
outcome, They honestly try for a
foundation and fight against the
tangents that would lure them away
from the necessity for building.
They seek knowledge for the sake
of its value and the enlighten-
ment it will bring them rather
than for satisfaction of idle cu-
riosity. If they are willing to
learn by experience and profit by
information gained, success is as-
sured.

Not often well suited for mar-
riage, the secret wish is there
and the experiment usually made.
If married, there are apt to be se-
cret jealousies and suspicions as
well as a change in their own feel-
ings.

They never remain in the place
of birth; they never stay long in
the same school or finish the course
they begin; they never adhere to the
same line of business-- or if they
do, they make such radical changes
in it that it is unrecognizable.

They must have an outlet for
their natural mental keeness and
the expression of their opinions.
The better the educational back-
ground, the more likelihood there
is for success, They have no set
creed or religion and what they de-
vise for themselves is never satis-
fying.

Peace of mind comes from the
willingness to accept life as it
must be lived-- constructively.

-77-

Challenge for the 5 C

SKEPTICISM

Birthdates Ruled by the 5 C

Mar. 31,
Aries.

Apr. 29.

Tau.

May 27.

Ruler- Mars.

Very mental birthdate.
Impulsive and progress-

ive. Often pioneers in lit-
erature or philosophy. Have
artistic and musical talent
and could make a great suc-
cess by cultivating it. Are
often careless about keeping
agreements. Are subject to
injustice from others. Are
not well adapted to law or
politics. Should have an oc-
cupation that assures a liv-
ing; no speculation. Should
avoid jealousy in personal
relationships. Can train
young people and become good
leaders if remain impersonal,
Ruler- Venus.

Artists, sculptors, fi-
nanciers and philanthro-
pists belong here. May be-
come very popular as leaders
of groups or projects. Have
a greater sense of protect-
ion and responsibility than
many 5 C, Secretive regard-
ing their affections and per-
sonal life. Want to live
well. If not talented in
some line, should have an
artistic outlet or interest,
Need harmony in surroundings.
Apt to be absorbed and ab-
sent-minded.

Ruler- Mercury.

Keenly interested in fi-
mance and may become fi-
nanciers themselves. Regard
the making of money as a fas-
cinating (and profitable)
game, so willing to stay with
it. Penetrating minds and in-
terested in people-~ but im-
personally. Hate and fear in~
security. Writers, journal-
ists, correspondents.

June 25.
Can.

July 23.
Can. or
Leo.

Aug. 21.
Leo,

Ruler- The Moon

Home very important.

Like all 5 C, restless

and eager for changes, but
always want roots and have
home on their minds while
traveling. Ally themselves
with groups but remain some-
what aloof. Interested in
social problems and reli-
gion; often engage in insti-
tutional work and remain be-
hind the scenes. Insistent
upon comfort and like te be
waited on. Should follow an
intellectual pursuit rather
than mechanical or commer-
cial, although many are bank-
ers and merchants. More tra-
ditional than other 5 C.
Ruler- The Moon or Sun

More drive for power

and prestige than June

25, Want recognition and
leadership. Not satisfied
with small returns for their
efforts. Much depressed by
temporary failure. Must cul-
tivate patience; can then
overcome obstacles. Often
give up when on the brink of
success. Are capable of mak-
ing big money if persistent.
Brokers, lawyers, merchants,
writers. Can also succeed in
the theatre but will abandon
it if fail to reach the top,
Ruler- The Sun

Must be at the head of

job or profession and

want to be considered an au~
thority in their field. Are
creative and original-- also
careful and methodical, Apt
to be skeptical, but keep on
investigating. Easily upset;
worry; borrow trouble. Valu-
able in the educational field.
May lack self-discipline but
are strict with others. Can
teach, publish, write. Have
a sense of duty and are pro-
testive toward those weaker.
Eager for truth and wisdom.

## Page 83

FIVE OF DIAMONDS

Diamonds - Values
5D - Fluctuation in Finan-

ces.

5 in D - Values clarified by
Contracts and Spiritual Un-
derstanding.

The Neptune Card in the Saturn L,
Displaces the 9 D in the Nat. Sp.

This Saturn-Neptune "con junc-
tion" appears, on first thought,
to be an irreconcilable combina-
tion, The idealistic, spiritual
yearnings of Neptune are apparent-
ly brought to a short stop by the
relentless materialism of Saturn.
That is, indeed, the outcome in
the lives of many of these natives.
We must bear in mind, however,
that Neptune is a gas (or a fog)
and that while it does not pene-
trate through or break down a
mass of rock, it can go under,
around, over and above it-- and
completely obscure it.

The solution is given by the
True Place. This, too, is in the
Saturn Line but its position is
Mars. WORK yourself out of your
difficulties; keep your INITIATIVES
on the Neptune level; FIGHT for the
principles and ideals that are your
birthright and Saturn himself will
give you the reward for your ef-
forts.

This does not imply the wis-
dom of trying to escape reality;

that can never be done with success.

It simply means overcoming the res~-
traints, frustrations and material
pressure of Saturn by substituting
a determined self-development and
spiritual awareness which are in
the gift of Neptune. There is the
same type of conflict in all cards
in this position; with the 5 D we
have the uncertainty of financial
security to contend with and the

constant temptation to yield to
expediency.

The Cross of this 5 is the
burden imposed by decision about
values. Not all of these natives
are lacking in financial security
-- although at some period of the
life there will be limitations;
the restrictions may come through
health or a hampering physical
affliction; through uncongenial
or troublesome children; through
a loved one who is faced with tri-
als that cannot be shared or
through an environment that is in-
harmonious to efforts for self-im-
provement.

5 D must choose their course
and stick to it. They must seek
a location where they can forget
themselves and make a contribution,
They must abolish fear, worry and
uncertainty. They must guard a-
gainst a tendency to dominate.
They must teach, preach and live
the true values they intuitively
know.

More than the other 5's, the
5 D has a sense of obligation to-
ward family and dependents. They
are also less selfish and more
considerate. The life is not an
easy one but victory is assured
through the development of their
own soul-power.

Money-consciousness is strong.
When it is regarded as a means,
not an end, it is usually at their
disposal when needed. Changes are
many; they seldom live near the
place of birth. Health problems
are diffuclt to diagnose-- and
seldom solved by orthodox, medi-
cal means, Personalities are im-
portant and contacts necessary.

If a woman, there is usually help
from a sympathetic husband, broth-
er or father.

-81-

counseling; they can become
"Kings" in their own right.
Investments are safer than
in the earlier years and a
permanent place can be es-
tablished without fear of
being uprooted, The men are
very successful in dealing
with groups; the women often
develop an interest in pub-
lic and community projects
and may have a voice in their
management,

May work in or for foreign
countries. Much travel is
indicated-- especially for
the men. Creative ability

is stimulated in the later
years and these people often
gain a high point of success
that was earlier denied them.
For those who have always
lived negatively or careless-
ly, the closing days of life
are less fortunate. Finances
are uncertain and friends
may be few. They usually
find themselves far from
home.

Challenge for the 5 D
SUBLIMATION OF REALITIES

Birthdates Ruled by the 5 D

Jan.

Aquar.

22. Ruler-

Uranus.

This is a constructive

and powerful birthdate--
especially if the work en-
gaged in has a wide appeal;
backed by a concept of uni-
versality. Many are attract-
ed to the entertainment
field, but are not at their
best there. If success is
gained, their inner longings
remain unsatisfied. 22 is
the number of the "Master
Builder"; any work that tax-
es their full capacity must
be both practical and ideal-
istic. Dislike changes that

Feb, 20.

Pisc.

Mar.
Pisce.

18.

interfere with their deter-
mination to build for per-
manence. Their knowledge

is used intuitively-- often
"dictated" from higher sour-
ces. Are hard workers but
dislike routine. Musicians,
poets and dramatists may
become famous. Usually have
some form of bondage to con-
tend with-- illness or af-
fliction of self or family,
financial limitation or a
type of service that keeps
them overworked. Can suc~
ceed in international af-
fairs.

Ruler - Neptune.

Mystical, poetic and mu-
sical. Should avoid lazi-
ness and getting into a rut.
If interested along spirit-
ual lines, make good healers
and practitioners. Can suc-
ceed at nursing, medicine or
hotel management. May reach
a high place as musicians
(especially stringed instru-
ments), dancers or singers.
The women have strong sense
of service unless too self-
centered and operating under
the QD.

Ruler - Neptune

More positive and univer-
sally minded than Feb. 20.
Have a gift for writing
which is not always recog-
nized by themselves. The
most unselfish of the 5 D;
apt to submerge themselves
in service. Should develop
self-sufficiency and less
self-sacrifice. Good trav-
elers, artists, philosoph-
ers, composers. Good for-
eign correspondents, pub-
lic servants. If any plan-
ets in Fire may become fam-
ous as leaders for causes.
Should not narrow their
field of activity to home
interests. Need to culti-
vate impersonality.

=83-

Sept. 6. Ruler- Mercury

Vir. Experts at research. At-
tracted to work that deals
with health measures and im-
provements in living condi-
tions. Investigating minds.
Interested in mental proces-
ces and make good psycholog-
ical theorists-- better than
counselors. Nervous and im-
patient; not good teachers
except for adult or co-in-
vestigators, Will accept res-
ponsibility from a sense of
duty but are easily bored by
it. Hate to be distracted
from their work. If a woman,
will give up work when she
marries. Both sexes approach
everything from a mental an-
gle-- art, literature or
the theatre.

Oct. 4, Ruler- Venus.

Lib. Most self-indulgent of the
5 D. Want diversion and es-
cape from responsibility,
Will make no effort to suc-~
ceed unless interested or
greatly benefitted. Should
guard against triviality and
inconsequentiality. Are eas-
ily influenced by their as-
sociates, so should choose

them with great care. Need
a good example in youth and
a training that will instil
stability. Are good company
and good (temporary) compan-
ions, The men often marry
for money or security. The
more constructive ones are
aware of the power and ad-
vantage of the 4 in their
birthday number. Can succeed
in music, writing, art or
the theatre, Make good trav-
eling salesmen.

Nov. 2. Ruler- Mars.

Scor. Success through con-
centration. Good sense of
values, good sportsmanship,
careful about obligations
and dutiful toward loved
ones. May inherit money but
if dependent upon own ef-
forts, are seldom adequate-
ly paid. Highly intuitive.
Usually attracted to meta-
physics and occultism, Want
to know reasons and causes,
Are good inventors, physi-
cians-- often surgeons.

Can succeed in the theatre

or in business. If negative,
become selfish and inconsid-
erate, "Talent'' for sarcasm.

AS ROARS ARS ACASATAY
5 OF SPADES
Spades - Labor; Service. or a disaffection with the envi-
5S - Crosses in Labors of ronment or the people that belong
Love. to them. They primarily want
5_in S - Opportunity through change for the sake of improve-
Change. ment-- not alone for themselves

The Mars Card in the Venus L.
Displaces the 10 H in the Nat. Sp.

The restlessness inherent in
all 5's assumes a different qual-
ity in Spades. Here it is not so
much a question of dissatisfac-
tion, a personal urge for freedom

but for their loved ones.

The Cross of the 5 S comes
through their affections. They
are seldom fickle or disloyal,
usually love deeply and perma-
nently, It is those they love
who bring the anxiety and heart-
ache. No sacrifice is too great
in their behalf, no service too

Birthdates Ruled by the 5 S.

Jan.
Cap.

9.

-85-

Work best in partnership

and friendly cooperation,
Gain through foreigners and
foreign interests, publica-
tion, wide distribution, etc.
In the case of a close part-
nership, it is best to let
the partner take the lead.
Business judgment is apt to
be uncertain and impractical.
Apt to have an agreeable
association or connection
with hospitals, institutions
or places of confinement. In
case of illness are usually
well cared for. Profit can

be made from business connec~
ted with supplies for doctors,
nurses, medicines, etc, Bene-
fit is likely through connec-
tion with governmental inter-
ests-- diplomacy, secret ser-
vice, bureaus, etc.

Strong attraction for the
eccult and psychic. Usual-

ly have intuitional power and
should cultivate it. Are well
adapted for dealing with fra-
ternities, lodges and orders.
Should seek to own property.
Not likely to do much trav-
eling after 55. The latter
years usually peaceful and se-
cure; should mot seem monoto-
nous-- even to the Aries birth-
date-- for there is ample op-
portunity to pursue the learn-
ing they have lacked and needed.

Feb. 7.
Aquar.

Pisc.

Apr. 3.

Challenge for the 5 S
DISCOURAGEMENT

May 1.
Tau.

Ruler- Saturn.

Merchandising the most pro-
fitable. Well adapted for
public life or a governmental
position. More ambitious for
place and power than other 5
S. Interested in economics,
government finances and man-

March 5.

agement of civic and commu~
nity projects. Believe in
"controls" and regimentation,
Personally ambitious but will
make sacrifices in private
life for a worthy cause.
Ruler- Uranus.

Averse to routine, Nervous,
Broad and tolerant view-
point. Have talent for music
which should be cultivated;
can develop great skill in
stringed instruments. Inter-
ested in human problems and
progress. Can succeed in real
estate, Apt to take many jour-
neys for business. Want per-
sonal freedom. Fine writers.
Ruler- Neptune.

Artistic and poetical.

Prefer art, music and lit-
erature to business, but can
succeed in oils, perfumes,
shipping and distant commerce,
Restless but less energetic
and determined than other 5 S.
Are often philanthropic and
universally minded. Sponsor
educational projects, move~
ments for the improvement of
hospitals, jails, etc.
Ruler- Mars.

Make excellent promoters

and salesmen-- if they

have faith in the article.
If inclined to metaphysics
will go far, Sense of drama;
are good speakers and convin-
cing in arguments. Latent tal-
ent for art-- especially dec-
oration, furniture, architec-
ture. Good taste, good judg-
ment. Can write or teach.
Ruler- Venus,

Home important and necess-
ary for happiness-- but

want to rule it. Set in opin-
ions. Fine writers-- usually
in serious vein, essays, phil-
osophy, etc, Women often have
fine voices; dramatic person-
ality. Meet with many changes
but dislike them. Can succeed
in any artistic profession.

## Page 91

SIX OF HEARTS

Hearts - Love.
6 - Sacrifice for Loved Ones.

6 in H - Cosmic Love.

The Mars Card in the Mars L.
Displaces the 4 C in the Nat. Sp.

This is a very stable and de-
pendable 6-- affectionate and emo-
tional but seldom swept off their
feet by their feelings. The dis-
placement of the 4 C assures them
of a certain amount of mental bal-
ance and good judgment-- IF they
choose to exercise it.

There is a tendency to be ra-
ther easy-going and the love of
ease, comfort and harmony often
interferes with making any mark
in life that involves a struggle.
They are humanitarian and self-
sacrificing, but they sometimes
disregard their Mars position and
their Club displacement and stay
by the fireside instead of brav-
ing a cold world. The men are in-
clined to be rather more active
than the women.

All 6 Hearts have come to
express and to teach the Law of
Love. They know that "love is
the fulfilling of the law" (Rom.
10:13) and they also know that
they must love in order to be
loved-- an important thing for
all Hearts.

Through the power of their
affections they can overcome all
difficulties; when they depart
from their law they are unhappy.
There can be no “eye for an eye,
tooth for a tooth" for these na-
tives. They must forgive all in-
juries, cancel all debts and still
"love the sinner", They are trus~
tees-- not owners-- of their mon-

ey. This is the Christmas Card;
they are bearers of pifts-- and
as a rule they enjoy being Lords
and Ladies Bountiful.

While always protected, they
like to make money themselves
and usually have little difficul-
ty in so doing. They are frequent-
ly found, however, in some chari-
table or institutional work where
their services are contributed or
their salaries negligible. The
work they are doing or the pro-
jects in which they are interested
are more important than the re-
turns. They like to live well
and they want money at their dis-
posal, but usually for the sake
of freedom in giving and sharing.

They should strive for a good
education. They have no difficul-
ty in learning but they do not
always retain or profit by what
they learn.

They dislike changes, Home
is important and once the sur-
roundings are established, they
want to keep them as they are.
If called upon to travel, they
set up a temporary home as they
go-- often loaded down with para-
phernalia and familiar gadgets
which make them feel at home.
Family pictures are always in
their pockets, family love in
their hearts.

Unless loving negatively--
that is, selfishly-- they are
comfortable, delightful people
to know. The faults to overcome
are criticism, domination and a
tendency to take charge of the
affairs of others and run them
in their own way. They are good
managers, but should wait to see
if their management is wanted.

=89-

The latter years are well
protected by love, faith-

ful friends and an easy life.
Here is every opportunity
for the fulfilment of cher-
ished ideals. Travel is well
favored and companionship is
obtainable if desired. There
may develop an idealistic
platonic friendship that adds
to happiness. The Law of Love
becomes very easy to express
and raise to the level of u-
niversality. Those of simi-
lar interests are drawn to
them and great spiritual de-
velopment is usually found
in these later years-- all
the more surely if the goal
has been set earlier.

Challenge for the 6 H
HUMILITY

Birt tes Ruled by the 6 H

Oct. 29. Ruler- Mars

Scor. An easier card for a wom-
an than a man. The women
may be less concerned with
"the world, the flesh and the
devel" and often become cos-
mic mothers. Both sexes are
usually drawn to the occult,
ancient mysteries and meta-
physical teaching. The feel-
ings are intense, the critic-
al faculty strong. They should
strive for gentleness and tol-

orance. Apt to follow heal-
ing lines and can succeed

in them as a profession,
Astronomy, astrology, aero-
nautics, archeology -- all
that deal with the partial-
ly known are means to suc-
cess. Thorough investigators.

Nov. 27. Ruler- Jupiter

Sag. More self-interested than
the other 6 H birthdates;
more willing to compromise.
Have psychic power. May be
interested in two things at
once-~ and work at both, If
the job is commercial, will
turn to metaphysical inter-
ests at night. Less depen-
dent upon home and family.
Should follow inclination
to teach or may become in-
troverted and neurotic. Can
succeed as writers, publish-
ers or exporters.

Dec. 25, Ruler- Saturn.

Cap. Scientists, writers and
statesmen belong to this
card. Are natural philan-
thropists. Much concerned
with questions of public in-
terest, principles of govern-
ment, justice and the laws
that deal with it. Great
sticklers for principle and
law. Become pillars of the
church, model citizens, etc.
More tolerant and broad mind-
ed than many. Capricornians.
Sponsor established Causes.
Faithful and dependable.

a John the Baptist who has come
to prepare the Way for salvation.
There are many 6 C who are una-
ware of their important mission,
unwilling to take the time or
trouble to develop intuition---
which is their greatest gift---
and unable to separate their per-

The women have a strong
mother instinct and a de-
sire to be good wives and
helpmeets. The men have loy-
alty and devotion to family
interests but should guard
against being dominated by
some woman in close relation-
ship to them. Both sexes have
charm and friendliness. Mar-
riage is usually fortunate
and happy-- from an emotional
angle-- but the strong Saturn
emphasis on the card itself
is likely to manifest in some
form of trial for which nei-
ther side may be responsible.
In personal relationships they
should guard against taking
too much for granted.

(Note that this card is in
the Crown Line).

Success in occupation will
come through understanding of
human nature and application
of innate knowledge. Mental
pursuits are best~--education-
al, judiciary, political, etc--
or the educational aspect of
any given talent-- teaching,
lecturing or writing on the
subject, Both moral and mate-
rial obligations must be thor-
oughly discharged. Success in
dealing with groups. This is
a fraternity card.

Finances are protected and
affluence often attained.
Money can be made through psy~
chic or intuitional gifts,
even without any commercial
motive. Money should not be
allowed to take first place;
when it does, the peace of
mind is threatened and sel-
fishness develops. In all ca-
ses of "high calling" this is
4@ grave pitfall.

Here is another evidence

that the "initiate" ele~
ment is strong in these peo~
ple. Karmic relationships
and experiences are in their
pattern and there should nev~

3

e

>
a

H

er be any rebellion against
them. What comes must be ac~
cepted as their due, This is
often a physician's card, so
schooled in impersonality as
to seem hard-boiled and un-
sympathetic, despite the in-
ner urge for healing and ser-
vice. Overwork should be a-
voided lest the health be
broken down and the balance
threatened. Old in experi-
ence and old in wisdom, they
can be of immeasurable ser~
vice to their fellow man.
There may be two lines

of activity, equally at-
tracting, and difficulty in
deciding between them. When
the decision is made, the
one not selected for concen-
tration should become a hob-
by or avocation; there is u-
sually an element of talent
or latent ability that should
not be wasted. The right se-
lection is usually made un-
less the desire to stand well
with others or the sense of
expediency prevails. A ten-
dency to show favoritism or
cater to those of prominence
should be checked.

Unlike the other 6's,

the 6 C are often detach-

ed and possibly lonely in
the earlier years. This is
less evident as life progres-
ses. They want companionship,
but it must be with those of
intelligence and understand-
ing. If opportunities for
travel have been rare, they
are likely to be plentiful
after 50. Until their last
day on earth they retain an
interest in universal condi-
tions, higher thought, reli-
gion and philosophy and it
broadens and increases in
old age.

CULTIVATION OF INTUITION
